FROM [Common].[Message] AS [m]

SELECT TOP(1) [m].[CandidateId], [m].[CompanyId], [m].[IsReceivedEmploye]
FROM [Common].[Message] AS [m]
INNER JOIN [Candidate].[Candidates] AS [c] ON [m].[CandidateId] = [c].[CandidateId]
INNER JOIN [Job].[Jobs] AS [j] ON [m].[JobId] = [j].[JobId]
INNER JOIN [Job].[AppliedJobs] AS [a] ON [m].[CandidateId] = [a].[CandidateId]
WHERE ((([a].[JobId] = [m].[JobId]) AND ([m].[CompanyId] = @__companyId_0)) AND ([m].[IsDelete] = 0)) AND ([m].[IsReceivedEmploye] = 0)
ORDER BY [m].[SendingTime] DESC

29-Oct-2020 22:33:23.708 +06:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (100ms) [Parameters=[@__orderByJobs_CompanyId_0='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [tf].[JobId], [tf].[JobTitle], [tf].[CompanyId], CASE
    WHEN [tf].[IsActive] IS NULL
    THEN CAST(0 AS BIT) ELSE [tf].[IsActive]
END AS [IsActive], [tf].[PublishedDate], [tf].[ExpiredDate], CASE
    WHEN [tf].[ApprovalStatus] IS NULL
    THEN 0 ELSE [tf].[ApprovalStatus]
END AS [ApprovalStatus]
